\begin{document}
\maketitle
\noindent This file is the canonical, dated record of every change to the TFPT theory
development: new verification modules (\texttt{vN}), status changes, editorial passes and
infrastructure. It is maintained \emph{in the same change} as the work it records, and it is
also imported at the end of the \texttt{introduction} document. Module numbers \texttt{vN}
refer to \texttt{verification/vN\_*.py}; claim IDs refer to rows of
\texttt{verification/status\_ledger.csv}.
\fi

\ifdefined\ChangelogImported
\clearpage
\section*{Appendix: changelog}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Appendix: changelog}
\noindent The dated record of every change (canonical source: \texttt{changelog.tex}, also
compiled standalone). Module numbers \texttt{vN} refer to \texttt{verification/vN\_*.py}.
\fi

\subsection*{2026-06-22 (endgame round: the necessity of $H$ reduced to the order-4 CM selection, the QG metric sector characterized as the conformal-mode problem, $|\det E_8|{=}1$ and the $\mu_4$ commutation grounded in Lean: \texttt{v331}, \texttt{v332}, \texttt{FORM.MU4COMM.01})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v331\_necessity\_of\_H.py} (\texttt{QGEO.NECESS.01}, \mE/\mO).} The necessity companion to
  \texttt{v329}: a concrete Steklov (DtN) computation shows the seam $\Lambda{=}|k|{+}M_f$ commutes with the $\mu_4$
  clock \emph{iff} the four marks sit at the square ($\tau{=}i$) --- moving a mark off the square breaks $\Z_4$ and
  $[\rho,\Lambda]\neq0$.  The square has cross-ratio $2$ ($j{=}1728$), the unique $4$-config with an order-4
  automorphism (\vref{v214}/\vref{v267}), so $H\Leftrightarrow$ square $\Leftrightarrow\mu_4$ and ``necessity of
  $H$'' sharpens to: the raw dynamics places the four Gauss--Bonnet marks (\vref{v216}) at the order-4 CM point.
  Residual $=$ that dynamical selection.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v332\_qgamb\_metric\_sector.py} (\texttt{QGAMB.METRIC.01}, \mE/\mC/\mO).} The open metric sector
  of \texttt{QG.AMB.01} is characterized precisely as the Gibbons--Hawking--Perry conformal-factor problem: the
  conformal mode has a negative kinetic coefficient $-(D{-}1)(D{-}2)/4$ (${=}-\tfrac32$ at $D{=}4$), so the bare
  Euclidean measure diverges over it.  The obstruction is in the conformal/gauge direction, gap-insulated from the
  admissible sector (\vref{v330}/\vref{v76}); the only route is the conditional IDG taming (\vref{v304}), with the
  polynomial $R{+}R^2$ ghost as the control.  Open, but pinned to one named obstruction.
\item \textbf{\texttt{CartanDeterminants.lean} extended (\texttt{FORM.CARTAN.DET.01}, \mE).} The rank-8 holomorphy
  discriminator $|\det\mathrm{Cartan}(E_8)|{=}1$ ($E_8$ has one anyon, vs $D_8$'s four) is now proved principally and
  kernel-only: \texttt{cartanE8 * cartanE8inv = 1} by \texttt{decide} on the 8$\times$8 PRODUCT gives
  \texttt{IsUnit (det E8)} via $\det E_8\cdot\det E_8^{-1}{=}\det 1{=}1$ --- no 8! determinant, no
  \texttt{native\_decide} (Mathlib itself leaves \texttt{E\textsubscript{8}\_det = 1} a \texttt{proof\_wanted}).
\item \textbf{\texttt{Mu4Commutation.lean} (\texttt{FORM.MU4COMM.01}, Lean 4, \mE).} The v201/v323 mark-locality
  criterion as exact linear algebra over the Gaussian integers $\Z[i]$: $i^4{=}1$, $i^2{=}-1$, and (on concrete
  $6\times6$ matrices) an offset-4 coupling commutes with the $\mu_4$ clock while an offset-2 coupling does not ---
  all by kernel \texttt{decide}.  Built \texttt{lake build} on Lean v4.29.1 $+$ Mathlib.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-22 (frontier round: the OS step discharged at the many-body level, the ambient measure built on the gap-decoupled sector, and the carrier Cartan determinants grounded in Lean: \texttt{v329}, \texttt{v330}, \texttt{FORM.CARTAN.DET.01})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v329\_os\_gap\_reduction.py} (\texttt{QGEO.OSGAP.01}, \mE/\mO).} The one analytic input the v308
  keystone chain still cited --- ``the OS-reconstructed bulk gap $=$ the transfer gap'' --- is discharged at the
  many-body level: the OS/Euclidean Hamiltonian is the second quantization $d\Gamma(-\log T)$, whose spectrum is the
  set of sums of single-mode energies, so the bulk gap $=$ the smallest positive single-mode energy $=6\ln\tfrac32$,
  \emph{independent of system size}.  Together with $H\Rightarrow\omega\circ\rho{=}\omega$ and $H\Rightarrow$ SRE
  $\Rightarrow(E_8)_1$, this exhibits the rotation-invariant flat-pillowcase premise $H$ as the \emph{single
  sufficient premise} of both bedrock IDs; residual $=$ the necessity of $H$ on the raw collar.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v330\_qgamb\_admissible\_measure.py} (\texttt{QGAMB.MEASURE.01}, \mE/\mO).} The constructive
  step \texttt{v275}'s roadmap calls for: on the gap-decoupled \emph{admissible} sector the ambient measure is built
  as a bona fide OS object --- reflection-positive (symmetric PSD transfer), exponentially clustering
  ($C(n)/C(n{-}1)\to(2/3)^6$), with finite susceptibility $\chi=729/665$ so $\mathrm{Var}(S_\Lambda)/\Lambda\to\chi$
  converges $\Rightarrow$ uniform tightness (Prokhorov) $\Rightarrow$ the projective limit exists; OS reconstruction
  gives $H_{\mathrm{OS}}\ge0$ with gap $6\ln\tfrac32$.  The full $\mathrm{QG}_{\mathrm{amb}}$ (the metric sector)
  stays open, gap-decoupled --- a genuine \emph{partial} construction, not a closure.
\item \textbf{\texttt{CartanDeterminants.lean} (\texttt{FORM.CARTAN.DET.01}, Lean 4, \mE).} The carrier piece of the
  holomorphy/anyon discriminator is grounded in real \texttt{Matrix.det} computations (kernel \texttt{decide}, no
  extra axiom): $|\det\mathrm{Cartan}(A_3)|{=}4{=}|\mu_4|$ (3$\times$3, \texttt{det\_fin\_three}) and
  $|\det\mathrm{Cartan}(D_5)|{=}4$ (5$\times$5, \texttt{decide}), giving the carrier $|\det\mathrm{Gram}|{=}4\cdot4{=}16$
  (the \texttt{v281} anyon count).  The rank-8 $E_8/D_8$ case stays the Nat discriminator --- Mathlib's own
  \texttt{Data.Matrix.Cartan} leaves \texttt{E\textsubscript{8}\_det = 1} as a \texttt{proof\_wanted}.  Built
  \texttt{lake build} on Lean v4.29.1 $+$ Mathlib.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-22 (next-steps round: the keystone collapsed to one shared premise (Lean $+$ one citable theorem), the $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ solver suite, the cusp weight derived from a minimal rewrite, and the $\theta_{13}$ pressure point: \texttt{FORM.QGEO.BW.01}, \texttt{v325}, \texttt{v326}, \texttt{v327}, \texttt{v328})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{BWKeystone.lean} (\texttt{FORM.QGEO.BW.01}, Lean 4, \mE/\mO).} The \texttt{v323} Bisognano--Wichmann
  linkage formalised: the nodes $\textsf{RotationInvariantVacuum}\to\textsf{GeometricModularFlow}\to
  \textsf{Mu4ModularSymmetry}\to\textsf{StateInvariance}$ (=\texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}) composed over the \texttt{v308} chain.
  The theorem \texttt{bedrockReducesToRotationInvariance} shows the WHOLE bedrock \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01} reduces to
  the SINGLE shared open premise \texttt{RotationInvariantVacuum} --- the two open bedrock items collapse to one ---
  with \texttt{\#print axioms} confirming the residual $=$ the cited chain steps $+$ recovery gap $+$ the named BW
  steps $+$ that one premise.  Plus a \texttt{decide}-proven discriminator $(1\mid4)\wedge\neg(4\mid1)$ (BW geometric
  flow strictly stronger than \texttt{v309} clock invariance).  Built \texttt{lake build} on Lean v4.29.1 $+$ Mathlib.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v325\_pillowcase\_keystone.py} (\texttt{QGEO.KEYSTONE.01}, \mE/\mO).} The keystone as ONE
  citable theorem: IF the raw seam state is the flat $\tau{=}i$ pillowcase (rotation-invariant) state THEN the whole
  bedrock closes (4 square marks, $\mu_4$ deck, $\omega\circ\rho{=}\omega$, holomorphic $c{=}8\Rightarrow(E_8)_1$,
  with the recovery gap as input); all pieces machine-checked (incl.\ the pillowcase $\chi_{\mathrm{orb}}{=}0$), the
  single open lemma shared by both bedrock IDs and Lean-pinned.  An assembly certificate, not a closure.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v326\_ftransfer\_suite.py} (\texttt{FR.SUITE.01}, \mE/\mC).} The four $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$
  readouts productised into one runnable harness, each a gapped relaxation to a unique attractor: $F_{\mathrm{pole}}$
  (Koide, seam rate $(2/3)^6$), $F_{\mathrm{Boltzmann}}$ ($\eta_B$, H-theorem), $F_{\mathrm{relic}}$ (axion adiabatic
  invariant), $F_{\mathrm{QCD}}$ ($m_p/m_e$, RG to the UV fixed point), plus the $F_{\mathrm{RareKaon}}$ bridge.
  Only $F_{\mathrm{pole}}$ carries the seam rate; the four external rates are honestly fenced (\texttt{v187}/\texttt{v303}).
\item \textbf{\texttt{v327\_hypergraph\_rewrite.py} (\texttt{HYP.REWRITE.01}, \mE/\mO).} The cusp weight $2/3$ is
  DERIVED from a minimal rewrite: a 3-channel/1-absorbing family rule has spectrum $\{1,2/3,0\}$, so
  $2/3{=}(\Nfam{-}1)/\Nfam{=}|\Z_2|/\Nfam$ emerges from the rule arity and $(2/3)^6{=}64/729$ is the recovery gap;
  with a PROOF that $2/3$ is not a root of the affine-$E_8$ charpoly ($p(2/3){=}-3520/19683\ne0$, sharpening \texttt{v312}).
  \texttt{v324}'s injected datum is reduced to the anchor arity $\{2,3\}$.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v328\_theta13\_pressure.py} (\texttt{FLAV.TH13.PRESSURE.01}, \mC/\mX) $+$ \texttt{v307}
  hardening.} The honest weak spot named and quantified: $\sin^2\theta_{13}{=}\phiz e^{-5/6}{=}0.023108$ is
  $+2.0\sigma$ above NuFIT 6.0 NO, a SEPARATE carrier-trace channel (\texttt{v268}), not relieved by any
  freeze-respecting correction (RG $<1\%$, exponent $5/6$ exact), pre-registered as the kill.  The \texttt{v307}
  watchdog gains a data provenance/date check and the rare-kaon $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ bridge row.
\item \textbf{Wolfram mirror $285\to288$.} \texttt{v325} ($\chi_{\mathrm{orb}}{=}0$) and \texttt{v327} (rewrite
  spectrum $\{0,2/3,1\}$, $(2/3)^6{=}64/729$, and the non-graph-spectral proof) added to
  \texttt{tfpt\_readouts\_extension.wl}; \texttt{GATE.WOLFRAM.02} and the Wolfram README updated to $288/288$.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-22 (consistency + de-accretion editorial pass: current-state alignment across papers, website and ledger; no new modules)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Keystone naming reconciled to \texttt{SEAM.EQUIV.01}.} Following \texttt{v323}/\texttt{QGEO.BW.01}
  (the deck premise is downstream of the seam being a chiral net), the single named open keystone is now
  \texttt{SEAM.EQUIV.01} \emph{everywhere}, with \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01} stated as its \emph{downstream}
  conformal-deck face. The ledger row \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01} was updated (it no longer calls itself ``the single
  structural residual of the whole theory''; it now depends on \texttt{SEAM.EQUIV.01}/\texttt{QGEO.BW.01}), and
  the superseded ``\texttt{GATE.QGEO} open gate'' / ``two research gates $(U_{\mathrm{wall}})$ and
  $G_{\mathrm{metric}}$'' framing was replaced by the current $\text{Rest}=v_{\mathrm{geo}}\oplus G_{\mathrm{net}}
  \oplus F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ with the two structural items \texttt{SEAM.EQUIV.01} $+$ \texttt{QG.AMB.01}
  (intro status card, \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier}, \texttt{origin\_theory}, \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam},
  \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}, and the website).
\item \textbf{De-accretion: the sprint-by-sprint reduction history was moved to this changelog, where it belongs.}
  Several reader-facing sections had grown by accretion (each round appended a clause). They were rewritten to
  state the \emph{current} result once, with the round-by-round narrative left here: the introduction closure
  ledger (``honest bottom line'') and hard-reduction subsection; the \texttt{origin\_theory} ``residual
  inventory'' (the five ``Update/\ldots/Terminal'' passes collapsed to one current inventory); the
  \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam} Target-A Outcome; and on the website the FAQ ``What is still open?'', the
  \texttt{OpenGates} closing-condition block, the \texttt{papers.ts} research-contracts/red-team entries, the
  verification-DAG \texttt{qft} node, the glossary \texttt{G\_net} entry, the Rosetta lexicon, and the
  verification/review pages. No scientific content or \texttt{\textbackslash veri} citation was dropped; only the
  embedded version-stamp logs were removed.
\item \textbf{Stale facts corrected.} Version label \texttt{5.0}$\to$\texttt{v5.2} (intro, single-sourced via
  \texttt{\textbackslash TFPTversion}); Lean build \texttt{1886}$\to$\texttt{3357} jobs (\texttt{FORM.SEAMEQUIV.01});
  README Python suite \texttt{v213}/\,212$\to$\texttt{v324}/\,322 modules; Wolfram extension
  \texttt{269/269}\,/\,\texttt{249/249}$\to$\texttt{285/285} (README, website replication page,
  \texttt{zenodo\_description.html}); residual ``Paper-3'' old-paper attributions in \texttt{tfpt\_2} neutralised.
\end{itemize}
\noindent\emph{(Original 2026-06-22 entry follows.)}

\subsection*{2026-06-22 (external-review pass: a registry bug fix, the NA62 2026 rare-kaon update, CP-phase prose hygiene, and three firewall/visualisation enhancements: \texttt{v202}, \texttt{v203}, \texttt{v305}, \texttt{v307}, \texttt{v321})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Bug fix --- $\delta_{\mathrm{CKM}}$ display value.} The predictions table (\texttt{tex-artefacts/predictions.tex})
  showed $\delta=\tfrac\pi3+3\lambda^2=66.96^\circ$, but that formula evaluates to $68.65^\circ$ (the canonical
  frozen \texttt{DELTA\_CKM\_RAD}$=1.198232$ rad, used by \texttt{v88}/\texttt{v202}/\texttt{FLAV.CP.01}
  everywhere else). Corrected to $68.65^\circ$. An external review correctly flagged the inconsistency; it was an
  isolated display typo (the website was already clean).
\item \textbf{\texttt{v202\_rare\_kaon.py} --- NA62 2016--2024 update (\mE/\mC).} The charged-mode comparison is
  moved from the historical NA62 $2016$--$2022$ observation $(13.0^{+3.3}_{-3.0})\times10^{-11}$ ($\sim1.2\sigma$
  above) to the full $2016$--$2024$ combination $\mathrm{BR}(K^+)=(9.6^{+1.9}_{-1.8})\times10^{-11}$
  (La~Thuile~2026), on which the prediction $9.45\times10^{-11}$ lands at $+0.08\sigma$. Framed honestly: a strong
  \emph{consistency} hit for the closed CKM point, but an $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ bridge --- \emph{not} a unique
  TFPT-vs-SM discriminator (the SM $(8.6\pm0.4)\times10^{-11}$ is also inside the NA62 error). Propagated to the
  ledger (\texttt{FR.RAREKAON.01}), \texttt{freeze\_file} (new \texttt{rare\_kaon} kill row), the watchdog
  (\texttt{v307}, a new $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ bridge row), the forward board (\texttt{v321}, rank 9), and
  \texttt{tfpt\_2\_standard\_model} $+$ the website.
\item \textbf{CP-phase prose hygiene.} The Galois CP lock is tightened from ``a relation to the \emph{measured}
  quark phase'' to ``a relation to the \emph{leading} ($\pi/3$) component of the quark phase'': the lock is to the
  structural $\pi/3$, not the full measured $\gamma=\delta_{\mathrm{CKM}}^{\mathrm{lead}}+3\lambda_C^2\approx68.7^\circ$,
  so $\delta_{\mathrm{PMNS}}=240^\circ$ (not $248.7^\circ$). Fixed in \texttt{tfpt\_2\_standard\_model},
  \texttt{origin\_theory}, \texttt{papers.ts} and \texttt{predictions.ts}.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v305\_witness\_independence.py} --- the No-Golden-Dynamics rule (\mE).} The number-field
  split is made an explicit anti-numerology firewall rule: $\phi=2\cos(\pi/5)\in\mathbb Q(\sqrt5)$ is the
  \emph{static} carrier ($\Z/5$) field, every \emph{dynamic} rate is rational ($\mathbb Q$, the $\Z/6$ hand), so a
  dynamic rate explained by $\phi$ is a cross-field false friend (\texttt{v314}/\texttt{v315}).
\item \textbf{\texttt{v203\_eht\_achromatic.py} --- the $\mu_4$ Fourier fourth null (\mX).} The EHT residual
  pre-registration gains a fourth null: the azimuthal residual must carry power \emph{only} at $m\equiv0\bmod4$
  (the $\mu_4$ fingerprint of the four marks, \texttt{v201}); a $\mu_4$-orbit profile has $\sim0$ off-mode power
  while a $\Z_2$ control leaks at $m=2$.
\item \textbf{Seed-hyperplane figure (Fig.~\ref{fig:seed-hyperplane}).} A new figure visualises \texttt{v306}:
  every scorecard observable inverts \emph{independently} to the one latent seed $\varphi_0$, the error-weighted
  mean matching the axiom to $0.04\%$, with $\sin^2\theta_{13}$ the $\sim2\sigma$ pressure point. Added to
  \texttt{make\_figures.py}, \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam} and the manifest.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-22 (Wolfram mirror of the arithmetic arc $+$ three sharpening steps: the CP-lock made quantitative, the Bisognano--Wichmann keystone, the minimal hypergraph fibre: \texttt{v322}, \texttt{v323}, \texttt{v324})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Wolfram mirror of the cyclotomic/Galois arithmetic arc (the independent second path).} The exact
  algebraic results of the arc are now mirrored in \texttt{verification/wolfram/tfpt\_readouts\_extension.wl} (ten new
  \texttt{checkExact} blocks, $275\to285$, \emph{all passing}): \texttt{v313} (the affine-$E_8$ characteristic
  polynomial with the golden factor $x^2{-}x{-}1$; the $(2,3,5)$ atoms as
  $2\cos(\pi/k)$; the $31/30$ selection), \texttt{v314} (the rational kernel vs $\mathbb Q(\sqrt5)$
  dynamic-rate split), \texttt{v315} ($30{=}5{\cdot}6$, $\varphi(30){=}8$, the Galois group $\mu_4\times\Z_2$, the
  $\sqrt5$ Gauss sum), \texttt{v316} ($\rho{=}\zeta_6{=}\zeta_{30}^5$, $\rho^4{=}-\rho$, $\mathrm{Gal}{=}\Z_2{=}$ CP
  conjugation), \texttt{v317} ($\Nfam{=}3$ as the $\mu_3$ orbit, the $1{+}2$ Galois split), \texttt{v318}
  ($\phiz{=}(4/3)\cthree{+}48\cthree^4$ a pure function of $\pi$) and \texttt{v320} (the CP lock
  $\delta_{\mathrm{PMNS}}{=}240^\circ$). Ledger \texttt{GATE.WOLFRAM.02} and the Wolfram README updated to $285/285$.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v322\_cp\_lock\_sharpened.py} (\texttt{GALOIS.CP.SHARPEN.01}, \mE/\mC/\mX).} The \texttt{v320}
  CP-lock sharpened into a quantitative, pre-registered kill test. \mE\ the leading phase sits on the six hexagonal
  nodes $\arg\rho^k{=}k\cdot60^\circ$, and \emph{which} one is selected is the deck order:
  $\delta_{\mathrm{PMNS}}^{\mathrm{lead}}{=}|\mu_4|\,\delta_{\mathrm{CKM}}^{\mathrm{lead}}{=}4(\pi/3)$ (node $4$);
  \mC\ the sub-leading correction is bounded by the quark analogue $3\lambda^2\approx8.7^\circ$, so the prediction is
  the band $240^\circ\pm\sim9^\circ$; \mC\ against NuFIT~6.0 (NO, $\delta_{CP}{=}212^{+26}_{-41}{}^\circ$) the leading
  value is $+1.08\sigma$, the band edge $+0.74\sigma$ -- compatible today; \mX\ the nearest wrong node is $60^\circ$
  away, far beyond the budget, so DUNE/Hyper-K ($\sim5$--$15^\circ$) discriminate cleanly. Cited in
  \texttt{origin\_theory}; ledger \texttt{GALOIS.CP.SHARPEN.01}.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v323\_bw\_geometric\_modular.py} (\texttt{QGEO.BW.01}, \mE/\mC/\mO).} The keystone pushed one
  honest step via Bisognano--Wichmann. \mE\ the $\mu_4$ clock is a geometric rotation
  $\rho{=}\mathrm{diag}(i^n){=}\exp(i\tfrac\pi2 L)$, $\mu_4\subset U(1)_{\mathrm{rot}}$; \mE\ for a rotation-covariant
  covariance $C{=}f(L)$ the modular Hamiltonian $K{=}\log((1{-}C)/C){=}g(L)$, so $[K,L]{=}0$ (the modular flow is
  geometric) and the clock is a modular symmetry \emph{for free} (the discriminator: a period-$4$ curvature preserves
  the clock but its flow is not geometric, $[K,L]\ne0$); \mC\ given the seam is the $(E_8)_1$ chiral net
  (\texttt{v308}), BW/Hislop--Longo make the vacuum modular flow geometric, so \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}
  ($\omega\circ\rho{=}\omega$) is \emph{downstream} of \texttt{SEAM.EQUIV.01} $+$ a rotation-invariant vacuum, not an
  independent axiom; \mO\ residual: the raw collar vacuum is rotation-invariant (cleaner than \texttt{v309}, shared
  with \texttt{v308}). Cited in \texttt{origin\_theory}; ledger \texttt{QGEO.BW.01}.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v324\_hypergraph\_fiber.py} (\texttt{HYP.FIBER.01}, \mE/\mC).} The constructive \texttt{v312}
  follow-up: the \emph{minimal} substrate that carries both the $E_8$ skeleton and the recovery gap is a
  \emph{product}. \mE\ the carrier network $T_{\mathrm{net}}{=}(A{+}2I)/4$ (attractor $=$ Kac marks $=$ skeleton)
  fibred by the $3$-node family cusp $T_{\mathrm{cusp}}{=}\mathrm{diag}((1{-}w)^{2\Nfam})$, $w\in\{0,\tfrac13,\tfrac23\}$
  (spectrum $\{1,(2/3)^6,(1/3)^6\}$); the fibred $T_{\mathrm{net}}\otimes T_{\mathrm{cusp}}$ has top eigenvalue $1$
  (eigenvector $\mathrm{marks}\otimes(w{=}0)$) and $(2/3)^6$ as a genuine eigenvalue ($\mathrm{marks}\otimes(w{=}\tfrac13)$)
  -- the $\Nfam{=}3$ cusp is the minimal fibre and the substrate $=$ carrier $\times$ family $=$ the
  $30{=}\gcar(2\Nfam){=}5{\times}6$ of \texttt{v315}; \mC\ honestly (\texttt{v312}) the cusp weight is still
  \emph{injected}, not derived from the graph -- a consistent realisation, not a derivation of $2/3$ from a pure
  rewrite. Cited in \texttt{origin\_theory}; ledger \texttt{HYP.FIBER.01}.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-22 (the forward kill-test board: the decisive upcoming measurements ranked, each locked to a freeze row --- incl. the new Galois-CP relation: \texttt{v321})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v321\_killtest\_board.py} (\texttt{KILL.BOARD.01}, \mE).} The forward companion to \texttt{v307}
  (the current-data board): the decisive \emph{upcoming} measurements, ranked and each locked to a

  $D_F$.} \mE\ $M_\nu=-m_D M_R^{-1} m_D^\top$ is symmetric, seesaw-suppressed and (for $\mu\tau$-symmetric

\subsection*{2026-06-17 (The Modular Spectral Closure: Dirac as covariance induction, the modular cutoff, the Kummer/K3 unification, and the assembly certificate, \texttt{v258}--\texttt{v261})}

\item \textbf{\texttt{v258\_dirac\_covariance\_induction.py} (\texttt{PS.DIRAC.03}) closes the

  Gaussian state is fixed by its covariance $C$ (a positive contraction) with one-particle modular
  Hamiltonian $H=\log((1{-}C)C^{-1})$ (Araki; Casini--Huerta), inverse to the KMS occupation
  $C=(1{+}e^{H})^{-1}$. \mE\ the inversion identity holds exactly; \mE\ $C_F$ is a positive contraction;
  \mE\ the induced operator is chirality-odd; \mE\ it is unitarily equivalent to the \vref{v252} $D_F$ (same
  mass spectrum); \mE\ the Majorana/seesaw $m_D^2/M_R$ is an off-diagonal covariance entry. \mC\

  K_{\mathrm{car}}]$ of the boundary geometry and the \vref{v18} Yukawas are the readout of $C_\Sigma$.

\subsection*{2026-06-17 (CP phases as $\mu_6$ powers --- a reduction of red-team Target D)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Both CP phases are $\mu_6$ powers of one hexagonal CM unit, split by the sheet
  (\texttt{v231\_cp\_mu6\_phases}, \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam}, \mE/\mC).} Sharper than \vref{v220}/\vref{v225}

  Eisenstein CM unit): $\delta_{\mathrm{CKM}}$ leading $=\arg(\rho^1)=\pi/3$ (quark) and
  $\delta_{\mathrm{PMNS}}=\arg(\rho^4)=4\pi/3$ (lepton, the phase lattice), with $\rho^4=-\rho$, so

  dual-frame Jarlskog orientations are sheet-flipped ($\pm21\sin(\pi/3)$). A structural reduction of Target~D
  (removes one of its two phase inputs); the quark seam correction $3\lambda_C^2$ stays the \vref{v88}
  misalignment, the deck stays $\Z/4$, and the physical CP derivation stays \mC\ (\texttt{CP.MU6.01}).
\item \textbf{The seam as the $E_8$ Kleinian singularity (\texttt{v232\_e8\_kleinian\_seam},
  \texttt{origin\_theory}, \mE/\mC).} The du~Val side of the McKay correspondence (\vref{v219}) gives the
  open seam-realisation premise \texttt{QGEO.REALIZE.01} a canonical algebraic-geometric model: dropping the
  trivial-rep node of the affine-$E_8$ McKay graph of $2I$ leaves the finite $E_8$ Dynkin $=$ the dual
  intersection graph of the eight exceptional $\PP^1$'s of the minimal resolution of $\mathbb C^2/2I$; the
  eight curves $=\operatorname{rank}E_8=g_{\mathrm{car}}{+}\Nfam$ (a fourth reading of the $8$), their negated
  intersection form is the $E_8$ Cartan ($\det1$, even, $(-2)$-curves), and the link is the Poincar\'e
  homology $3$-sphere $S^3/2I$ ($2I$ perfect $\Rightarrow H_1{=}0$, $\pi_1{=}2I$ order $120$). The raw seam
  ($\PP^1$ with marks)   is canonically a du~Val exceptional curve --- a model for the bedrock, not a P2 proof
  (it presupposes $E_8$; \texttt{TOPO.E8.01}, bedrock stays \mO).
\item \textbf{CP is the universal family/triality phase, only sheet-split
  (\texttt{v233\_cp\_triality\_phase}, \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam}, \mE/\mC).} One step past \vref{v231} in the
  $\mu_6=\mu_3$(family/triality)$\times\mu_2$(sheet) factorisation: $\rho=\omega^2(-1)$ with $\omega=e^{2\pi i/3}$
  the $\Z_3$ triality centre (the $2/3$ cusp weight). Since $\rho^4=\rho^1\rho^3$ with $\rho^3\in\mu_2$, the
  quark ($\rho^1$) and lepton ($\rho^4$) CP phases share the \emph{same} family/triality class and differ only
  by the sheet --- so CP \emph{is} the universal triality phase, sheet-split, not a free power choice
  (\texttt{CP.TRIALITY.01}).
\item \textbf{The Seam-Holomorphy selection certificate: the structural residual is one gate
  (\texttt{v234\_seam\_holomorphy\_selection}, \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}, \mE/\mO).} The whole
  structural residual is \emph{one} condition --- ``the seam carries no nontrivial abelian sector'' --- with
  three provably-equivalent faces, all forcing $E_8$: (i) holomorphy ($\mu$-index $1$; Target A), (ii) the
  seam link is a homology $3$-sphere ($\Gamma$ perfect $\Leftrightarrow2I$; \vref{v232}), (iii) exactly one

  for $E_8$; and holomorphic $c{=}8{=}\gcar{+}\Nfam$ gives the unique even unimodular rank-$8$ lattice $E_8$.

  (\texttt{v235\_seam\_chern\_simons}, \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}, \mE/\mO).} A genuine reduction

  one integer condition ``the free RP seam condenses the Lagrangian glue ($\det{=}1$)'' $=$ the sheet/QGEO

  $E_8$, not a P2 proof (\texttt{MCKAY.E8.01}).

\subsection*{2026-06-15 (the diamond axis geometry --- two axes + the transfer corner)}

  the decuple then the full generation (identity \mE, source$\to$pole reading \mC). \textbf{(3) Spectral

  $(1,3,4,6)$ and kernels $(13,48,65,105)$, $F$ carrying $105=3{\cdot}5{\cdot}7$. The anchor-defect
  spectrum and pair-sum/staircase blocks are honest \emph{audit} fingerprints ($28{=}2\dim G_2$,

\subsection*{2026-06-15 (bedrock: the $\omega\circ\rho=\omega$ residual reduced once more --- v201)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{QGEO.SUBPRIN.01} (\vref{v201}, \mE/\mO).} The \vref{v199} bedrock residual --- ``the
  bounded sub-principal symbol of the raw seam DtN has no off-character (mod 4) matrix elements'' --- is
  reduced one genuine step further: block-diagonality is \emph{not} an independent postulate. Writing the
  DtN as $\Lambda=|k|+M_f$ with $M_f$ the bounded sub-principal piece $=$ multiplication by a curvature
  $f(\theta)$ (standard Steklov structure), $M_f$ is $\mu_4$-character-block-diagonal iff $f$ is
  $\Z_4$-invariant (\mE; principal $|k|$ already commutes, \vref{v198}); and a $\mu_4$-mark sum
  $f=\sum_{j=0}^3 g(\theta-2\pi j/4)$ has $f_m=4g_m[m\equiv0\bmod4]$ for any profile $g$, hence is
  automatically $\Z_4$-invariant (\mE). So the $\mu_4$-mark orbit (forced by \vref{v195}) \emph{forces} the
  sub-principal symbol block-diagonal; $3$ marks ($\Z_3$) and $4$ generic marks break it (negative
  controls). The residual collapses to ``the DtN sub-principal symbol is mark-local (seam flat away from the
  $\mu_4$ marks $=$ conformal deck, \vref{v177})'', structurally definitional --- the narrowest form yet of
  \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}, \mO. Registered in \texttt{run\_all.py}, the ledger, \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts},
  \texttt{origin\_theory}; Wolfram-mirrored (the mark-sum Fourier identity is exact; extension now
  $242/242$). Suite $200$ modules.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-15 (F\_transfer workshop: the axion relic solver --- an honest over-production tension)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Axion relic solver (\texttt{experiments/ftransfer/axion\_relic/relic\_solver.py}, \mC).} The
  first real $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ pipeline computation (work package C / review \S6.2): a standard
  misalignment relic with a numerically-computed anharmonic factor $F(\theta_i)\approx4$ at the hilltop.
  Honest finding: at the \emph{predicted} $\theta_i\approx170^\circ$ the estimate \emph{over}-produces dark
  matter, $\Omega_a h^2\sim0.6$--$2.3$ (robustly $>0.12$), because the large $\theta_i^2\approx8.8$ times $F$
  overshoots. So the determinant-line axion as the \emph{dominant} DM is in \emph{mild tension} (it would
  prefer $\theta_i\sim120$--$130^\circ$ or extra dilution) --- this \emph{refines} \vref{v185}'s optimistic
  ``can be all-DM'' toward an over-production tension. The near-hilltop regime is O(1)-uncertain, so a full
  finite-$T$ solve decides; over-production kills only the axion-as-dominant-DM \emph{branch}, not the
  compiler. Reflected in \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier} (dark-matter section) and the \vref{v185} docstring;
  experiments-only, not a suite/ledger claim. No refitted exponents; $\theta_i=\pi(1-\varphi_{\mathrm{seam}})$
  only.
\item \textbf{Full finite-$T$ solve confirms it (\texttt{axion\_relic/full\_finiteT\_solve.py}).} A converged
  nonlinear misalignment solve ($\theta''+(3+\mathrm{d}\ln H/\mathrm{d}N)\theta'+(m_a(T)/H)^2\sin\theta=0$,
  lattice $\chi(T)\propto T^{-8.16}$, realistic $g_*(T)$; normalised so $\theta_i{=}1\to\Omega_a h^2\approx0.03$,
  the standard value) gives $\Omega_a h^2\approx0.66$ at the predicted $\theta_i\approx170^\circ$ ---
  $\sim$5.5$\times$ above $\Omega_{\mathrm{DM}}=0.12$, reached only at $\theta_i\approx106^\circ$. The
  over-production is thus \emph{confirmed} (not the optimistic ``all-DM''); \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier},
  \vref{v185} docstring and the website updated accordingly. Stays \mC; kills only the
  axion-as-dominant-DM branch.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (work packages A+B: attacking $\omega\circ\rho=\omega$ + the variational scan --- v199, v200)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v199\_seam\_state\_invariance.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.STATE.01}, work package A).}
  Attacking $\omega\circ\rho=\omega$ directly on the \emph{raw} seam. (1) \mE\ the setup is non-circular:
  $\rho$ is the Coxeter element of $W(A_3)=S_4$ ($\rho^4=1$, \vref{v117}), an automorphism of the raw CAR
  algebra (16 Majoranas) --- both carrier-side, no seam geometry. (2) \mE\ for a quasi-free RP state
  $C_\Sigma=\tfrac12(1{+}\operatorname{sgn}H_1)$, so $\omega\circ\rho=\omega\Leftrightarrow[\rho,H_1]=0$.
  (3) \mE\ $[\rho,H_1]=0\Leftrightarrow H_1$ is block-diagonal in the four $\mu_4$-character classes
  $\{n{=}r\bmod4\}$ (verified). (4) \mO\ the residual is sharpened to ``the bounded sub-principal symbol has
  no off-character matrix elements'' --- a bounded, finite-character condition, not a diffuse geometry; not
  a closure. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}; Wolfram-mirrored.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v200\_seam\_variational\_scan.py} \mC/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.VARI.02}, work package B).}
  The discretised variational test: with the clock angle free, $E_{\mathrm{fail}}(\theta)$ has its unique
  minimum at $\theta=\pi/2$ (the $\mu_4$ clock $z\mapsto iz$) --- order-4 \emph{and} the three distinct
  characters $i,-1,-i$ = the $(1,2,3)$ grading; decoys ($0,\pi,\pi/3,2\pi/3$) all lose. A numerical sign
  that the variational principle selects $\mu_4$; the full operator-valued minimisation stays the
  \vref{v199} residual \mO. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}.
\item \emph{Also (this pass, \texttt{experiments/} only, not the ledger): the $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$
  four-pipeline scaffold (\texttt{experiments/ftransfer/}) with one CONTRACT per interface, and confirmation
  that the FRB preregistration (\texttt{frb\_tfpt\_v1.yaml}) and its status semantics already exist.}
  Suite now 199 modules, highest ID \texttt{v200}; Wolfram extension $241/241$.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (cracking the bedrock to a state-invariance: principal symbol $+$ Tomita--Takesaki --- v198)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v198\_modular\_commutator\_reduction.py} \mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.MODULAR.01}).} The
  decisive crack on the last residual. (1)~\mE\ the DtN principal symbol
  $|k|=\sqrt{-\partial_\theta^2}=\mathrm{diag}(|n|)$ and the clock $\rho{:}z\mapsto iz=\mathrm{diag}(i^n)$ are
  both diagonal in the Fourier basis, so $[\rho,|k|]=0$ \emph{exactly} on all of $L^2$ (verified on 33
  modes) --- the leading-order commutation is free on the whole boundary, never the open part. (2)~\mE\ by
  Tomita--Takesaki the modular operator is intrinsic to $(M,\Omega)$, so a state-preserving symmetry
  ($\rho\Omega=\Omega$) commutes with $\log\Delta\sim\Lambda_\Sigma$: hence $[\rho,\Lambda_\Sigma]=0$
  \emph{follows from} $\omega\circ\rho=\omega$, using only the state $+$ reflection (RP) and \emph{no}
  conformal covariance --- which \textbf{removes the v194 Bisognano--Wichmann circularity worry}. (3)~\mE\
  the finite $H^1$ block is already $\mu_4$-invariant (\vref{v177}). So the entire residual collapses to the
  single \emph{state-invariance} ``the raw quasi-free seam state is $\mu_4$-invariant''
  ($\omega\circ\rho=\omega$ $\Leftarrow$ the Gaussian bulk measure is deck-invariant) --- the
  maximally-operational, non-circular form of \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}, \mO. \emph{Not} a full closure (a
  foundational symmetry cannot be derived from nothing, like $c=\text{const}$), but the sharpest falsifiable
  form, with the circularity gone. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}; \texttt{OpenGates} updated.
  Suite now 197 modules, highest ID \texttt{v198}; Wolfram extension $240/240$.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (three review levers: Marks-via-Lefschetz, E\_fail functional, RR$\to$D5 --- v195--v197)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v195\_marks\_lefschetz\_character.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.MARKS.02}).} The four
  seam marks are \emph{forced} (not posited): $\rho{:}z\mapsto iz$ fixes only $\{0,\infty\}$, $H^1=
  \chi_1{\oplus}\chi_2{\oplus}\chi_3$ (the $A_3$ exponents, $\operatorname{Tr}(\rho|H^1)=i{+}i^2{+}i^3={-}1$)
  has no trivial component $\Rightarrow$ no puncture at a fixed point, and $\operatorname{rank}H^1=n{-}1=3
  \Rightarrow n=4 \Rightarrow$ a single free $\mu_4$ orbit (cross-ratio $2$). So \textsc{Marks} reduces from
  the geometric posit ``$D_4$ marks'' to the milder premise ``$H^1$ carries the $A_3$-exponent rep'' ---
  less circular, still \mO. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v196\_seam\_energy\_functional.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.VARI.01}).} The
  failure functional $E_{\mathrm{fail}}=\|[\rho,\Lambda_\Sigma]\|^2_{HS}+\|\rho^4{-}1\|^2+\|\Theta\rho\Theta-\rho^{-1}\|^2$,
  zero locus $=$ the \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01} conditions; on the finite $H^1$ block it vanishes at the $\mu_4$
  config \mE\ and is $>0$ for any $\mu_4$-breaking perturbation, so $\mu_4$ is a true minimiser. The
  full-operator minimisation is the \vref{v194} Bisognano--Wichmann residual --- a concrete discretisable
  \emph{target} on the open bedrock, \mO. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v197\_rr\_carrier\_clifford\_d5.py} \mE/\mC\ (claim \texttt{ARCH.RRCAR.02}).} Hardens
  the Riemann--Roch carrier from $g_{\mathrm{car}}$ to $D_5$ itself: $\Lambda^{\mathrm{even}}(C_{\mathrm{car}})
  =\binom50{+}\binom52{+}\binom54=16=2^{g_{\mathrm{car}}-1}=\dim S^+$, the $\mathfrak{so}(10)=D_5$
  half-spinor --- so $D_5$ is the Clifford spinor of the $5$-dim mode space, closing $\mu_4{\to}g_{\mathrm{car}}{\to}D_5$.
  \mE\ arithmetic, \mC\ identification (as \vref{v189}). Cited in \texttt{origin\_theory}.
\item All three are validated external-review levers (the axion-hilltop ``$\pi-3\phi_0$'' proposal was
  \emph{rejected} as a $\pi\approx3$ coincidence, not built). Suite now 196 modules, highest ID
  \texttt{v197}; Wolfram extension $239/239$.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (operator origin of the Koide 53/54 factor: the missing Sheet-Diamond corner, v183)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v183\_koide\_f\_corner\_transfer.py} \mE/\mC\ (claim \texttt{FR.KOIDE.07}).} An
  external-review proposal, validated exactly: the Koide source$\to$pole factor $\tfrac{53}{54}$ is not
  a bare arithmetic guess but an \emph{operator} identity on the carrier,
  $u_{\mathrm{pole}}/u_{\mathrm{source}} = a^T(R+Q)\mathbf1 / (2\,\mathbf1^T R a) = 53/(2{\cdot}27) =
  \tfrac{53}{54}$. Here $\mathbf1^T R a = 27$ is the $E_6{\times}A_2$ cubic family block
  ($248 = \dim E_6 + \det R + 2(\mathbf1^T R a)\Nfam = 78+8+2{\cdot}27{\cdot}3$) and
  $a^T(R+Q)\mathbf1 = 53 = 52+1$, where $F = R+Q$ is the \emph{missing} Sheet-Diamond corner with
  $\det B_F = 52 = \dim F_4$ (\vref{v80}). Hard negative control: $a^T M\mathbf1$ for $M\in\{R,Q,K,L\}$
  is $\{32,21,35,56\}$ --- only the absent corner $F$ gives $53$. This upgrades \texttt{FR.KOIDE.03}
  from ``near miss $+$ conjecture'' to ``operator-sourced source$\to$pole transfer'': the \emph{factor}
  is \mE\ (exact, mirrored in Wolfram, $232/232$); the \emph{mechanism} (the leptonic source$\to$pole
  transfer reads the $F$ corner) stays \mC, an $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ special case. The prediction
  itself stays \mC. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier} (Koide section). Suite now 183 modules.
\item \textbf{Review point 2 noted as already-present:} the claim that flavor and Nariai share one
  double-cover ClockFunctor (flavor rate $(2/3)^{2\Nfam}$ vs gravity curvature $(2/3)^{\Nfam}$, exponent
  ratio $|\Z_2|$, ``one clock, two geometries'') is exactly \texttt{HOR.TRISECT.01}/\vref{v103} --- a
  rediscovery of an existing result, no new module.

  open'' card; the achievement is that the whole theory is compressed onto exactly one sharply-located,
  falsifiable premise.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (the final reduction to bedrock v181 + full non-changelog status sweep)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v181\_clock\_is\_conformal\_symmetry.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}).}
  The isometry premise \texttt{QGEO.ISO.01} (\vref{v180}) is weakened one more genuine step --- to a
  conformal-\emph{symmetry} premise --- via \emph{equivariant uniformisation} (Nielsen realisation; for
  cyclic groups Ker\'ekj\'art\'o $+$ uniformisation): a \emph{conformal} automorphism (strictly weaker
  than an isometry --- every isometry is conformal, conformal allows any positive scale) already suffices
  to put the order-$4$ clock in the form $z\mapsto iz$. Since the clock is the Coxeter element of
  $W(A_3)=S_4$ (\vref{v117}), the $\mu_4$ deck, and a deck transformation preserves the pulled-back
  conformal structure by definition, the residual collapses to the \emph{definitional} identification
  \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}: ``the seam's conformal structure \emph{is} the $\mu_4$-deck structure of the
  carrier clock''. This is bedrock --- a physical/definitional statement tying P2 to the seam's conformal
  geometry, \emph{not} a finite computation and not reducible further without relabeling. The chain
  \texttt{REALIZE}(\vref{v175})$\to\dots\to$\texttt{SYM.01}(\vref{v181}) ends here; we stop honestly.
  Python-only. Suite now 181 modules.
\item \textbf{Full non-changelog status sweep.} The current bedrock framing was propagated to every
  live status surface (not just the changelog): the \texttt{introduction} ``latest reductions'' prose,
  \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam} Target~A, the \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts} central-theorem keybox,
  \texttt{origin\_theory}; and on the website \texttt{OpenGates}, \texttt{VerificationDag},
  \texttt{papers.ts} (Target~A $\times2$, $G_{\mathrm{net}}$), the \texttt{glossary} $G_{\mathrm{net}}$
  entry and the \texttt{faq} live-residual answer --- all now end at \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (the conformal premise reduces to a milder isometry premise v180)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v180\_clock\_is\_mobius.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.ISO.01}).} Cracks
  \texttt{QGEO.CONF.01} one level further: the conformal-realisation premise is \emph{replaced}, via
  three classical theorems, by a strictly \emph{milder, non-circular} premise. (1)~\emph{Uniformisation}
  (Poincar\'e--Koebe): a genus-$0$ Riemann surface is conformally $\PP$, so the genus-$0$ seam double
  (P1, \vref{v179}) with its RP-metric conformal structure \emph{is} $\PP$ --- the target is
  \emph{produced}, not assumed; (2)~\emph{Ker\'ekj\'art\'o} (1919; Constantin--Kolev 2003): a
  finite-order orientation-preserving homeomorphism of $S^2$ is conjugate to a rotation, so the
  order-$4$ clock ($h(A_3){=}4$) is topologically $z\mapsto iz$; (3)~\emph{isometry$\Rightarrow$
  conformal$\Rightarrow$M\"obius}: an orientation-preserving isometry of a Riemannian surface is
  holomorphic, $\mathrm{Aut}(\PP)=\mathrm{PSL}(2,\mathbb C)$; (4)~an order-$4$ M\"obius map is
  $z\mapsto iz$ (verified: projective order $4$, fixed $\{0,\infty\}$, multiplier $i$, free orbit
  $\mu_4$). Hence \texttt{QGEO.CONF.01} is \emph{implied} by the milder premise \texttt{QGEO.ISO.01}:
  ``the carrier clock is an order-$4$ orientation-preserving \emph{isometry} of the RP seam metric'' ---
  which does not name $\PP/\mu_4$ (uniformisation produces them) and is the natural statement that the
  seam transport is metric-compatible (a holonomy preserving the RP inner product). That milder premise
  is the single, now milder, structural residual of the whole theory; its surface realisation from the
  raw seam stays honestly \mO. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}; Python-only. Suite now 180
  modules.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (the two obligations collapse to ONE geometric premise v179)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v179\_conformal\_realisation.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.CONF.01}).}
  Investigating the two residual premises left by \vref{v178} shows they are \emph{not} independent ---
  they collapse onto a single geometric premise (honest unification; the premise itself stays \mO).
  \textsc{Marks}'s residual is not three independent assumptions: (1)~genus-$0$ \emph{is} P1 --- the
  one-sided Gauss--Bonnet $c_3=1/(|\Z_2|\,2\pi\,\chi(S^2))=1/(8\pi)$ uses $\chi(S^2)=2$ and
  $\chi=2-2g\Rightarrow g=0$, so ``genus-$0$'' is the same $\chi=2$ that gives the ``$8$'' in $c_3$
  (\vref{v58}/\vref{v73}); (2)~the order-$4$ clock \emph{is} the carrier --- the Coxeter element of
  $W(A_3)=S_4$ (\vref{v117}), order $h(A_3)=4=|\mu_4|$; (3)~marks $=$ one orbit is \emph{forced} (the
  parabolic marks are not the two elliptic fixed points, a free order-$4$ orbit has exactly $4=e_1(a)$
  points). \textsc{Kernel} then \emph{follows} from the same geometry (DtN symbol $|k|$, Lee--Uhlmann
  \vref{v156}; $c=8$ rigidity \vref{v158}; the cusped-surface residual $=H^1=\mathbb C^3=\Nfam$). So
  the \emph{entire} structural residual of the theory is the \emph{single} geometric premise
  \texttt{QGEO.CONF.01}: ``the raw RP seam normal double is conformally $(\PP,\mu_4)$ with the carrier
  clock as the order-$4$ M\"obius automorphism''. The two doors of \vref{v177}/\vref{v178} are one
  geometric realisation, left honestly \mO. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}; Python-only.
  Suite now 179 modules.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (an honest attempt at the two obligations v178 --- deeper reduction, not closure)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v178\_marks\_kernel\_attempt.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.REDUCE.01}).} An
  honest attempt at \texttt{QGEO.MARKS.01} and \texttt{QGEO.KERNEL.01}. These are genuine
  constructive-geometry/AQFT statements, \emph{not} finite computations --- neither is closed. What
  the module does is push each as far as computation allows: it closes the finite \mE\ core of each
  and reduces each to \emph{one sharper} premise. \emph{Marks core} \mE: given a genus-$0$ double with
  an order-$4$ clock $\rho$ (fixed points $\{0,\infty\}$) and reflection $\tau$, the marks are forced
  to be a generic $\rho$-orbit $\{1,i,-1,-i\}=\mu_4$ (\emph{not} the fixed points), distinct iff
  $b_1=4-1=3=\Nfam$ (any collision drops $b_1$), with $\tau\rho\tau=\rho^{-1}$ giving a faithful $D_4$
  of order $8$ --- so \textsc{Marks} reduces to the single topological/clock premise. \emph{Kernel
  core} \mE: on the $3$-dim multiplicity-free $H^1$ the $\mu_4$ characters $(1,2,3)$ are distinct, so
  by Schur a $\mu_4$-equivariant operator is forced \emph{diagonal} and completely determined by its
  eigenvalue per character; two such with the forced transfer spectrum $\{1,(2/3)^6,(1/3)^6\}$
  (\vref{v162}) and the unique residue-normalised basis (\vref{v177}) are \emph{equal as operators},
  not merely isospectral --- the spectrum-vs-operator worry \emph{vanishes} on the finite block. So
  \textsc{Kernel} reduces to the single full-operator-reduction premise (principal symbol $|k|$,
  Lee--Uhlmann/\vref{v156}; no drift \vref{v158}). Net: neither obligation closed; both sharpened to
  milder premises with their finite cores \mE. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}; Python-only
  (M\"obius/Schur symbolic $+$ numeric). Suite now 178 modules.
\end{itemize}

  (empty-array expansion under \texttt{set -u}).
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (QGEO rigidity theorem v168 + $\eta_B$ leptogenesis interface v169)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v168\_qgeo\_rigidity.py} \mE/\mC{} (claims \texttt{QGEO.RIGID.01},
  \texttt{QGEO.REALIZE.01}).} Hardens the \emph{finite} half of the one remaining Tier-1 hinge
  \texttt{GATE.QGEO} (the seam $=$ flavour $=$ horizon identification). Exact, machine-checked:
  $\mu_4=\{1,i,-1,-i\}$ has cross-ratio $2$ and a faithful M\"obius stabiliser of order $8=|D_4|$;
  $H^1(\mathbb P^1\!\setminus\!\mu_4)$ has rank $4-1=N_{\mathrm{fam}}=3$; and the forms
  $\omega_k=z^{k-1}dz/(z^4-1)$ ($k=1,2,3$) are $\mu_4$-eigenforms with characters
  $\chi_1,\chi_2,\chi_3$ of weights $(1,2,3)=$ A$_3$ exponents $=\operatorname{Spec}(Q_+)$. So a
  genus-0 boundary with faithful $D_4$, four parabolic marks and this $\mu_4$-decomposition is
  M\"obius-equivalent to $\mathbb P^1\!\setminus\!\mu_4$ --- the QGEO Rigidity Theorem
  (\texttt{QGEO.RIGID.01}, \mE). The seam-collar realisation stays the one premise
  (\texttt{QGEO.REALIZE.01}, \mC). Mirrored in the Wolfram extension (226/226). Cited in
  \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts} (U0). \emph{Not} a new structural class --- it hardens the
  existing hinge (consistent with v167's completeness claim).
\item \textbf{\texttt{v169\_etaB\_boltzmann\_interface.py} \mC{} (claim \texttt{FR.ETAB.02}).}
  Operationalises the Tier-3 $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ leptogenesis path. Type-I thermal
  leptogenesis $\eta_B\sim0.96\times10^{-2}\varepsilon_1\kappa_f$ (sphaleron $28/79$), fed by
  TFPT's normal-ordered neutrino spectrum and the predicted $\delta_{CP}=240^\circ$. Over natural
  $M_1\in[3\times10^9,3\times10^{10}]$ GeV and washout, $\eta_B$ brackets the observed
  $6.1\times10^{-10}$ (a canonical point gives $6.0\times10^{-10}$, untuned) --- the route is
  \emph{viable}. But $M_1$/washout are scenario inputs, so $\eta_B$ stays \mC; if a precise solve
  excluded the window the leptogenesis \emph{route} falls, not the theory (the downstream
  $\Omega_b$ readout is independent). Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier} (Route B). Python-only.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (Higgs quartic from the free seam: SM near-criticality explained, v166)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v166\_higgs\_free\_seam.py} \mE/\mC{} (claim \texttt{HIGGS.FREESEAM.01}).}
  A new prediction tying the Higgs mass to premise~(A). The seam UV is the free chiral
  $c{=}8$ fixed point (v158, Gaussian, no relevant/marginal interactions), so the one
  marginal SM scalar coupling vanishes there: $\lambda(M_{\mathrm{seam}})=0$ and
  $\beta_\lambda(M_{\mathrm{seam}})=0$ --- the Shaposhnikov--Wetterich double-criticality,
  here \emph{derived} from the free seam, not assumed. Integrating the PyR@TE-confirmed
  \emph{two-loop} SM RGEs from $M_Z$ up with the measured $(m_H,m_t)$ gives
  $\lambda(\bar M_{\mathrm{Pl}})\approx0.002$ and $\beta_\lambda(\bar M_{\mathrm{Pl}})\approx0$:
  the famous SM near-criticality is a \emph{consequence} of the free seam (2-loop sharpens
  $\lambda(\bar M_{\mathrm{Pl}})$ from ${\sim}0.022$ at one loop to ${\sim}0.002$). The double
  condition predicts $m_H\sim129$--$134$ GeV; the same condition at the scalaron scale gives
  ${\sim}107$ GeV (too low), so the boundary condition lives at the reduced Planck scale
  (seam $=$ horizon $=$ Planck). Fills the Higgs-sector gap (was only $N_\Phi=1$); cited in
  \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier}.
\item PyR@TE-sourced: the reproducer's SM run supplies the two-loop $\beta_\lambda$, reduced
  to top-only (\texttt{verification/pyrate/sm\_higgs\_betas.txt}). Suite now 166 modules.
  Python-only (numerical 2-loop ODE).
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (PyR@TE $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ follow-ups: flavor scale-tagging v163, QCD scale v164)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v163\_rg\_stability\_flavor.py} \mE/\mC{} (claim \texttt{FLAV.RGSTAB.01}).}
  Scale-tagging of the flavor sector. The lepton-mixing seeds
  ($\sin^2\theta_{12}=\tfrac13-\tfrac{\varphi_0}{2}=0.3067$,
  $\sin^2\theta_{13}=\varphi_0 e^{-5/6}=0.0231$) are \emph{RG-stable}: the PMNS
  running is $y_\tau^2$-suppressed (the only mixing-rotating Yukawa term is
  $\tfrac32 Y_e Y_e^\dagger Y_e$, PyR@TE SM RGEs), so
  $\kappa_\tau=y_\tau^2/(16\pi^2)\ln(M_{\mathrm{scal}}/M_Z)\sim1.8\times10^{-5}$ and
  $|\Delta\sin^2\theta_{ij}|\lesssim10^{-4}$ --- two to three orders below precision.
  Seam value $=$ measured value; the $y_t^2$-driven quark mass ratios ($m_t/m_b\sim41$)
  by contrast carry a scale tag. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_2} (solar/reactor angle box).
\item \textbf{\texttt{v164\_qcd\_scale.py} \mE/\mO{} (claim \texttt{QCD.LAMBDA.01}).}
  The QCD confinement scale is parameter-free from the carrier $b_3=-7$ (v159):
  running $\alpha_s(M_Z)=0.1179$ down (two-loop, $n_f$ thresholds) reproduces
  $\alpha_s(m_b)\simeq0.22$, $\alpha_s(m_c)\simeq0.38$ and confinement at
  $\sim0.5$ GeV by dimensional transmutation --- so the QCD-scale \emph{numerator} of
  $m_p/m_e$ is independently sourced. The $O(1)$ proton/$\Lambda$ factor is lattice, so
  $m_p/m_e=1836$ stays the honest ``\mO\ --- not forced'' frontier ratio. Cited in
  \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier}.
\item Both are PyR@TE-backed (the reproducer now also extracts the SM Yukawa $\beta$'s,
  \texttt{verification/pyrate/sm\_yukawa\_betas.txt}). Suite now 164 modules. Python-only
  (no Wolfram mirror: magnitude bound / numerical running).
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (PyR@TE external cross-check of the $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ gauge inputs --- v159)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{New module \texttt{v159\_pyrate\_gauge\_crosscheck.py} \mE/\mC{} (claim
  \texttt{EM.BUDGET.02}).} The one-loop gauge coefficients used by the transfer functor
  are confirmed by an \emph{independent} third-party RGE generator. Feeding the carrier
  / Standard-Model field content into the textbook one-loop formula (GUT normalisation)
  gives $(b_1,b_2,b_3)=(\tfrac{41}{10},-\tfrac{19}{6},-7)$, and \textbf{PyR@TE\,3}
  (\texttt{arXiv:2007.12700}, \texttt{github.com/LSartore/pyrate}) writes
  $\beta_{g_1}=(\tfrac{41}{10})g_1^3$, $\beta_{g_2}=-\tfrac{19}{6}g_2^3$,
  $\beta_{g_3}=-7g_3^3$ verbatim (plus the full standard 2-loop matrix). So $b_1=41/10$
  is pinned \emph{three} independent ways --- carrier algebra
  $10b_1=\gcar 2^{\gcar-2}{+}1=41$, the $U(1)$ hypercharge index $\sum\tfrac35 Y^2$, and
  PyR@TE --- and the split $10b_1=40_{\text{(ferm.)}}+1_{\text{(Higgs)}}=41$ reproduces
  the EM-budget Gate~1 of \texttt{tfpt\_2}. Cited there with \texttt{\textbackslash veri};
  the gauge sector of $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ is thus not a free knob.
\item \textbf{PyR@TE reproducer (not vendored).} \texttt{verification/pyrate/reproduce.sh}
  clones PyR@TE on demand into \texttt{experiments/pyrate} (git-ignored), neutralises its
  interactive \texttt{pdflatex} end-command, runs the SM at one and two loops, and
  re-extracts the gauge $\beta$ functions; the committed evidence is
  \texttt{verification/pyrate/sm\_gauge\_betas.txt}. PyR@TE is the right external tool for
  the transfer/RGE gates (gauge running, and --- with a seesaw model --- the
  neutrino-Yukawa running behind $\eta_B$); it is \emph{not} a tool for premise~(A) (a
  2d boundary-CFT question). Mirrored in the Wolfram extension; suite now 159 modules.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (the final identification: premise A factors into the already-open A2 + R1, no new open content, \vref{v162})}

  symbol splits into a gap value $(\beta)$ and a fixed space $(\alpha)$. \textbf{$(\beta)$ is forced:} a
  $\mu_4$-equivariant generator is diagonal in the cusp basis (the deck average is the diagonal projection,
  $\sum_{k}U^kXU^{-k}=|\mu_4|\operatorname{diag}X$ for $U{=}\operatorname{diag}(1,i,-i)$; the commutant of
  $U$ is exactly the diagonal algebra), so its spectrum is the cusp weights
  $\operatorname{spec}(A_0^\star){=}\{0,\tfrac13,\tfrac23\}$ (\vref{v115}) and the transfer eigenvalue
  $(1{-}\alpha)^{p_2}$ with $p_2{=}6{=}|R_+(A_3)|$ gives $\{1,(2/3)^6,(1/3)^6\}$, gap $6\log\tfrac32$ ---
  all carrier data; the lift to the $16$ Majoranas is the $A_3$ subnet grading (\vref{v137}).
  \textbf{$(\alpha)$} is the rank-$8$ Calder\'on polarisation of $\omega_k{=}|k|$ (\vref{v113}/\vref{v156}).
  \textbf{Closure:} with \vref{v160}$+$\vref{v161}, (A) closes given only $\mu_4$-equivariance $+$
  admissibility, whose two non-derived inputs are the already-open A2 (net existence, Kawahigashi--Longo)
  and R1 (seam clock, \texttt{HOR.CLOCK}). So premise~(A) factors exactly into $A_2+R_1$ --- it adds

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (the cone reduces to one particle: premise A's scope premise discharged to a 16-dim statement, \vref{v161})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{New module \texttt{v161\_one\_particle\_reduction.py} \mE/\mO.} \emph{Discharges} the scope
  premise of \vref{v160} (``the transport is gapped on the \emph{full} Schwinger cone'') via Bogoliubov
  second quantisation. A quasi-free transport is $T_\Sigma{=}\Gamma(t)$, the second quantisation of a
  one-particle contraction $t$ on the $16$-dim Majorana space; $\Gamma(t)$ acts on the degree-$m$ correlator
  sector as the exterior power $\Lambda^m(t)$. Machine-checked: (1) $\operatorname{spec}(\Gamma(t)|_{\deg m})
  ={}$ products of $m$ one-particle eigenvalues (compound-matrix theorem, all $m{=}0..6$); (2) \textbf{the
  cone gap equals the one-particle gap} --- the sub-leading eigenvalue over the whole cone is $(2/3)^6$
  exactly, so premise~5 on the cumulant space \emph{is} premise~5 on the $16$-dim space; (3) the
  eigenvalue-$1$ sector is $\Lambda^{*}$ of the fixed subspace (disconnected Wick powers), with uniqueness
  closed by \vref{v113} (one polarisation $\Leftrightarrow$ one vacuum); (4) quasi-freeness is \emph{forced}
  --- the $120{=}\dim\mathfrak{so}(16)$ chiral currents are the Bogoliubov generators and \vref{v158} makes
  every non-Gaussian deformation irrelevant. \textbf{Consequence:} \vref{v160}'s three full-cone premises
  collapse to ONE finite ($16$-dim) one-particle statement (seam symbol $=$ gapped Calder\'on Bogoliubov
  map, fixed $=$ rank-$8$ $K_\Sigma$, gap $(2/3)^6$); all numbers supplied, only the physical identification
  (Kawahigashi--Longo class $=$ the A2 net residual) stays open --- the infinite-dimensional cone is
  eliminated (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.17}). Python-only (numpy $+$ stdlib).
\item \textbf{Bookkeeping.} Suite at $161$ modules, all green; Wolfram extension unchanged at $224/224$;
  \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts} (premise-A keybox) and \texttt{next.txt} moved together.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (premise A as a conditional fixed-point theorem; the load relocates to one scope premise, \vref{v160})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{New module \texttt{v160\_seam\_gaussianity\_from\_pf.py} \mE/\mO.} Formalises the proposed
  closure of premise~(A) (``the seam bulk is a reflection-positive free field'') as a fixed-point theorem
  and types it honestly. The \emph{exact} parts: (1) a quasi-free state has \emph{all} higher connected
  cumulants $\kappa_{2n}{=}0$ --- verified by the \emph{signed} set-partition/Pfaffian moment$\leftrightarrow$%
  cumulant inversion on a concrete pure Majorana covariance (the \vref{v113} ``one kernel $=$ net'' property
  at the cumulant level); (2) a kernel-preserving transport fixes the whole quasi-free state by Wick
  functoriality; (3) the Perron--Frobenius dichotomy (a \emph{fixed} $\kappa_{2n}$ is a second fixed ray
  $\Rightarrow$ breaks uniqueness; a \emph{non-fixed} one decays by the gap) forces Gaussianity; (4) the
  qualitative claim needs only $\mathrm{gap}{>}0$, the value $(2/3)^6$ only sets the rate. \textbf{The
  honest residual:} \vref{v56}'s gapped PF uniqueness lives on the \emph{three-dimensional} scalar transfer
  spectrum $\{1,(2/3)^6,(1/3)^6\}$, while the $16$-Majorana seam already carries $\binom{16}{4}{=}1820$ and
  $\binom{16}{6}{=}8008$ higher-cumulant directions --- so (A) reduces to the single internal, exact-testable
  statement ``the admissible TFPT seam transport is primitive $+$ spectrally gapped on the \emph{full}
  Schwinger cone, not only the readout spectrum of \vref{v56}'', which the suite does \emph{not} yet
  establish (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.16}). Python-only (numpy $+$ stdlib); no new exact-identity content
  for the Wolfram mirror.
\item \textbf{Bookkeeping.} Suite at $160$ modules, all green; Wolfram extension unchanged at $224/224$

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (premise A: the destination fixed point is provably stable, \vref{v158})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{The free chiral $c{=}8$ fixed point is provably stable (\vref{v158}, exact dimension count).}
  The finite core of (A)'s ``reaches-the-fixed-point'' residual: the chiral Majorana has $h{=}\tfrac12$,
  the bilinear current $h{=}1$, the quartic $h{=}2$. The relevant window $0<h<1$ for bosonic deformations
  is \emph{empty}, the $h{=}1$ currents are chiral (\vref{v157}, not $(1,1)$-marginal), and the lowest
  interaction (quartic, $h{=}2$) is irrelevant --- so the fixed point is isolated and stable against all
  interactions. Premise (A) reduces to a basin-of-attraction statement with a \emph{proven} stable target
  (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.15}). \emph{Tooling note:} PyR@TE (4d gauge-Yukawa RGEs) is the wrong tool
  for this 2d boundary-CFT residual, but the right tool for the $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ interfaces
  ($\eta_B$ leptogenesis RGEs, gauge-coupling running, the $b_1{=}41/10$ cross-check).

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (premise A reframed: freeness is a rigid boundary fixed point, \vref{v157})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{The free-bulk premise becomes a fixed-point property (\vref{v157}, simplicity-first).}
  Instead of postulating Gaussianity, three facts click: (i) the DtN/Calder\'on symbol is
  \emph{universally} $|k|$ (Lee--Uhlmann --- order-$1$ $\Psi$DO, principal symbol $|\xi|_g$;
  interactions live in the irrelevant lower-order symbol), so the free dispersion is
  bulk-detail-independent; (ii) a holomorphic $c{=}8$ theory is \emph{rigid} --- every field has
  $\bar h{=}0$, so no marginal $(1,1)$ field exists and the fixed point is isolated, with no knob for an
  interaction; (iii) the same $|\Z_2|$ that halves $8\pi$ in $\cthree=\tfrac1{8\pi}$ is the Ramond/GSO
  projection giving $\mu{=}1$ ($248{=}120_{\mathrm{NS}}{+}128_{\mathrm R}$). With $(E_8)_1$ unique
  (\vref{v83}), premise~(A) shrinks from ``prove the seam is Gaussian'' to ``the gapped
  ($\Delta{=}6\log\tfrac32$) boundary flow reaches the holomorphic fixed point'' --- freeness then forced
  by rigidity, not fine-tuned (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.14}).
\item \textbf{Bookkeeping.} Suite at $157$ modules, all green; Wolfram extension $223/223$;
  contracts / \texttt{origin\_theory} / \texttt{next.txt} / website moved together.

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (Route 3: the seam net constructed and $(E_8)_1$ verified, \vref{v156})}

  is no longer an assertion: the chiral seam net is built explicitly and the identification \emph{checked}.
  (a) The Dirichlet-to-Neumann (Calder\'on) operator of the $2$d Laplacian is the free chiral dispersion
  $\omega_k=|k|$ (harmonic extension $e^{ikx-|k|y}$); (b) $16$ free Majoranas give $c=8=5{+}3$; (c) the
  weight-$1$ currents are $248=120_{\mathrm{NS}}+128_{\mathrm R}$ ($SO(16)$ bilinears $+$ Ramond spinor,
  Frenkel--Kac); (d) the holomorphic character $E_4/\eta^8=q^{-1/3}(1+248q+4124q^2+34752q^3+213126q^4)
  =j^{1/3}$ (verified by $q$-series) --- the $248$ at level $1$ is $\dim E_8$, so the net \emph{is}
  $(E_8)_1$. \emph{Residual:} exact given (i) the free-bulk premise (DtN $=|k|$, \vref{v155}) and (ii) the
  operator-algebraic existence of the net from the seam kernel (a Kawahigashi--Longo-type theorem, not a

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (the seam-side identification reduced to one shared premise, \vref{v155})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{$G_{\mathrm{net}}$'s last premise reduces to a single shared physical premise
  (\vref{v155}, Python-only).} The seam-side identification of the Simple-Current Extension Theorem
  (\vref{v154}) splits (\vref{v110}) into (a) ``the Calder\'on involution is sheet-odd'' (the
  double-cover deck, structural) and (b) ``the seam $2$-point kernel is quasi-free''. Part~(b) is
  \emph{not} independent: the boundary marginal of a reflection-positive \emph{Gaussian} bulk is the
  compression $P\Gamma P$ of the covariance, and the compression of a contraction is a contraction ---
  so the seam state is automatically quasi-free (Wick inherited). Hence (b) \emph{follows} from ``the
  seam bulk is a reflection-positive free field'', the \emph{same} premise already load-bearing in the
  area law (\vref{v59}) and the EH mechanism (\vref{v150}/\vref{v151}). \textbf{The entire seam-side
  residual is therefore one physical premise}, shared by $G_{\mathrm{net}}$, the area law and R3 ---
  not reducible by a finite computation, but no longer three separate items (ledger
  \texttt{GATE.METRIC.12}).
\item \textbf{Bookkeeping.} Suite at $155$ modules, all green; Wolfram unchanged at $221/221$
  (\vref{v155} is numerical/numpy, Python-only); contracts / \texttt{origin\_theory} /
  \texttt{next.txt} / website moved together.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (external review formalised: No-Unit Theorem + Simple-Current Extension Theorem, \vref{v153}--\vref{v154})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{$v_{\mathrm{geo}}$ re-typed: the No-Unit Theorem (\vref{v153}).} Every load-bearing
  compiler datum is mass-dimension $0$ and invariant under a unit rescaling $L\mapsto\lambda L$,
  whereas a mass / $1/G$ is not --- so a dimensionless boundary compiler \emph{provably cannot}
  select an absolute scale. $v_{\mathrm{geo}}$ is therefore an \emph{irreducible metrology
  primitive}, not an open gap, and the three apparent residuals collapse onto it
  ($U_{\mathrm{point}}\sim v_{\mathrm{geo}}$, $1/G\sim v_{\mathrm{geo}}^2$, $m/\mu=e^{3/4}$ a pure
  ratio); the irreducibles stay $\{$one unit, $\pi\}$ (ledger \texttt{ANCHOR.VGEO.02}).
\item \textbf{$G_{\mathrm{net}}$ stated as the central closing theorem (\vref{v154}).} The Simple-Current
  Extension Theorem: $A{=}(D_5)_1{\otimes}(A_3)_1$ extended by the isotropic glue
  $L{=}\langle(1,1)\rangle$ has $[B{:}A]{=}|L|{=}4$, $c{=}5{+}3{=}8$,
  $\mu(B){=}\mu(A)/|L|^2{=}16/16{=}1\Rightarrow$ holomorphic $\Rightarrow B\cong(E_8)_1$ ($SO(16)_1$
  excluded). Every algebraic ingredient is machine-checked (\vref{v89}/\vref{v92}/\vref{v125}/%
  \vref{v143}/\vref{v148}); the only residue is the seam-side identification. Pulled to the front of
  \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}, \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam} (Target~A final form) and
  \texttt{origin\_theory} (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.11}).
\item \textbf{Status surfaces re-typed} (review): the canonical status card now reads
  $v_{\mathrm{geo}}$ as a metrology \emph{primitive}, $G_{\mathrm{net}}$ as the simple-current
  extension $\cong(E_8)_1$ (\mE/\mC), and $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ as one functor with four typed
  interfaces --- ``not structural gaps''. The final one-line framing (dimensionless boundary compiler;
  irreducibles $\{\pi, v_{\mathrm{geo}}\}$; one seam-net theorem; frontier $=$ $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$)
  is in \texttt{origin\_theory}, the introduction, the README and \texttt{next.txt}.
\item \textbf{Bookkeeping.} Suite at $154$ modules, all green; Wolfram extension $221/221$;
  intro/README/\texttt{origin\_theory}/contracts/redteam/status-card/website moved together.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (fifth round: the R3 normalisation is the dimensionful anchor, \vref{v152})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{R3: the $q(A_3)$ normalisation merges into the one anchor (\vref{v152}).} The
  replica EH coefficient is a \emph{log-ratio} $k=\ln(m/\mu)/(12\pi)$ ($\ln m$ alone is
  scale-ambiguous, only $m/\mu$ is physical); pinning $k=\cthree/2$ fixes the
  dimensionless ratio $m/\mu=e^{3/4}$, and in $d{=}2$ that ratio \emph{is} the induced
  Newton constant $1/G$ (\vref{v68}). So $v_{\mathrm{geo}}$ (\vref{v78}), $1/G$
  (\vref{v68}) and $m/\mu$ are \emph{one} dimensionful anchor in three readings --- the
  irreducibles stay $\{$one scale, $\pi\}$, and \texttt{SEAM.THEOREM.01}'s residual
  reduces to the kernel-identification premise alone. \emph{Audit (not promoted):} the
  log-ratio is numerically $\tfrac34=q(A_3)$, the target value the anchor takes in seam
  units --- not a derivation (ledger \texttt{SEAM.EHMODEL.03}).
\item \textbf{Bookkeeping.} Suite at $152$ modules, all green; Wolfram extension
  $219/219$; intro/README/\texttt{origin\_theory}/\texttt{next.txt}/website moved together.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-12 (R1--R5 second round: every class at its floor, \vref{v145}--\vref{v148})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{R4$'$: the pairing values are atom identities (\vref{v145}).} Reading the
  \vref{v139} lift structurally ($n=w_0(\sigma)+|\mu_4|e_3$, $w_0=$ the $A_3$ exponent
  duality), all three pairings become atom arithmetic --- including the \emph{new}
  closure $|\mu_4|+\gcar=\Nfam^2$ ($4{+}5{=}9$, $\sigma\perp w_0(a)$) and
  $\|\sigma\|^2=110=|\Z_2|\gcar\|\mathrm{Pl}(K)\|_1$. R4$'$ $=$ derive \emph{one} map
  (ledger \texttt{GATE.UWALL.13}).
\item \textbf{R5: the M\"obius $D_4$ realisation (\vref{v146}).} The \emph{full}
  dihedral symmetry $\langle z{\mapsto}iz,\,z{\mapsto}1/z\rangle$ of the seam curve acts
  on $H^1$ exactly as the integer model: $\iota^*$ is the exponent duality with parity
  $+1$ on the self-conjugate line ($=T_A$ in the cusp basis, glue-swap parity), and
  $\Sigma$ is the $\delta\iota$ class --- the premise reduces to the module
  identification itself (ledger \texttt{FLAV.QGEO.07}).
\item \textbf{R1: the clock is a Gaussian zero-mode integral, and the bend is
  det$'$-clean (\vref{v147}).} Variance ratio $(1-\alpha)$ (forced by norm $=$ area)
  gives the Born-squared ratio $(1-\alpha)^{p_2}$, the $\ln$ series \emph{is} the
  \vref{v127} ring sum; the two quantum weights share \emph{one} Nariai geometry, so the
  bend $\log_{3/2}3$ carries no determinant correction --- the \vref{v144} obstruction is
  localised to the $\alpha=0$ reference (ledger \texttt{HOR.CLOCK.13}).
\item \textbf{R2: the NS/R sector census (\vref{v148}).} The untwisted (Neveu--Schwarz)
  module carries only the \emph{even} discriminant classes (integer weights), so the odd
  $\mu_4$ simple currents have zero NS support --- they are Ramond modules; the R
  zero-mode module ($256$) splits $128{+}128$ into the odd sectors of the \emph{two}
  Lagrangian glues: choosing the glue \emph{is} choosing the R-projection
  ($248=120_{\mathrm{NS}}{+}128_{\mathrm R}$); the one remaining net statement is
  irreducibly twisted-sector (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.10}). \emph{Correction note
  (same day):} the first version of \vref{v148} graded the Ramond labels by the sum
  $q_D{+}q_A$ (not the glue label) and called that module untwisted; the census was
  rewritten as above --- conclusion unchanged, support corrected, the R-sector sheet
  split is new.

\subsection*{2026-06-12 (R1--R5 attack round: four residual classes sharpened, \vref{v141}--\vref{v144})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{R5 closed at the discrete level (\vref{v141}, deck selection theorem).} The
  \vref{v140} $\Z_3$ choice is \emph{derived}: the established integer deck $G=T_A\Sigma$
  (\vref{v97}/\vref{v98}) pairs the $Q_+{=}1$ cusp line with the self-conjugate character
  $2$, so only the sheet-twisted assignment $(2,3,1)=\mathrm{chars}(-U)$ survives; the cusp
  exponential $i^{Q_+}$ is excluded (same spectrum, wrong grading pairing). Explicit
  conjugacy constructed; under $k\to-k$ only the established sheet $\Z_2$ flips.
  Consequence: Euler grading $=Q_+\!\circ\rho$. \texttt{GATE.QGEO} keeps only its
  realisation premise --- no discrete freedom left (ledger \texttt{FLAV.QGEO.06}).
\item \textbf{R4$'$ narrowed: three pairings $\to$ two (\vref{v142}, frame integrality).}
  Integer covectors in the $(\mathbf1,a,\sigma)$ dual frame form an index-$11$ sublattice
  ($x-3y+z\equiv0$ mod $11$; the index \emph{is} $\|\mathrm{Pl}(K)\|_1$); with
  $(x,y)=(|\Z_2|,\mathrm{rank}\,E_8)$ the $\sigma$-pairing is forced $\equiv0$ mod $11$,
  and primitivity forces the line parameter even. Cramer reductions for both line pairings
  recorded as restructuring (ledger \texttt{GATE.UWALL.12}).
\item \textbf{R2 realised at the finite Lie level (\vref{v143}, graded Frobenius).} The
  $\Z_4$-graded hull carries exact coset duality ($-C_1=C_3$; Killing pairing nondegenerate
  per $g_k\times g_{-k}$), the glue average is exactly the carrier projector (index $4$),
  and each glue sector is one Weyl orbit (simple currents, fusion $=\mathbb C[\Z_4]$) ---
  the \vref{v125} Q-system realised by the hull; residue $=$ one conformal-net statement
  (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.09}).
\item \textbf{R1's det-ratio step derived in-family (\vref{v144}).} $e_2$-rigidity of the
  traceless SdS cubic gives $r_br_c=1-\Delta^2/3$ exactly; with the \vref{v132} anomaly the
  non-zero-mode determinant ratio is $(1-\Delta^2/3)^{4/3}$ --- no first-order term in the
  horizon split (the \vref{v131} cancellation derived, not assumed); deficit coefficient
  $\tfrac{32}{27}=|\mu_4|(\tfrac23)^3$ (audit). Finite-weight absorption stays \mC\ with the
  $6\to\tfrac{14}3$ obstruction stated sharply (ledger \texttt{HOR.CLOCK.12}).
\item \textbf{R3 attempted, honestly unchanged.} No defensible computation landed for the
  seam-determinant$\to$EH step (\texttt{SEAM.THEOREM.01}); the gate keeps its \mO\ typing
  untouched.
\item \textbf{Wolfram mirror extended} to \vref{v141}--\vref{v144}: extension file now
  $211/211$ (\texttt{GATE.WOLFRAM.02} and the wolfram README updated in lock-step); Python
  suite at $144$ modules, all green.
\end{itemize}

  sentence'', ``The unification'', ``The question and the honest answer'', ``Net: two axioms''); tfpt\_4
  from $18$ to $7$ (the seven-box Koide stack and the two dark-matter conjecture boxes become prose). The
  per-item ``Honest status of \ldots'' keyboxes are kept --- tfpt\_4 is the status authority for the
  frontier.
\item \textbf{Colour-marked module references.} \texttt{\textbackslash vref} applied to the inline
  \texttt{vN} references in tfpt\_3 and tfpt\_4 (TikZ node names excluded).
\item \textbf{Marker hygiene.} A stale literal \texttt{[P]} in tfpt\_4 (Koide flow-time) replaced by the
  4-class \mC; status tables checked against the ledger.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-12 (marker simplification to 4 classes + status reconciliation)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Four-class display markers.} The reader-facing marker system is collapsed from eleven
  symbols to four: \mE\ exact / machine-proven (identity, Lie/lattice, formalised, numerical FP),
  \mC\ conditional (physical / bridge / readout under named hypotheses), \mO\ open / axiom, and \mX\
  kill test. \texttt{tex-artefacts/tfpt\_style.tex} defines \texttt{\textbackslash mE/\textbackslash
  mC/\textbackslash mO/\textbackslash mX} and keeps the legacy \texttt{\textbackslash tI \ldots
  \textbackslash tX} names as aliases that render their class. All marker call-sites across the nine
  documents and the shared fragments were rewritten, collapsing same-class combinations (e.g.\
  \texttt{[I]/[L]}\,$\to$\,\mE, \texttt{[N]/[P]}\,$\to$\,\mE/\mC). The fine-grained per-claim type
  (Axiom / Formal / Lattice / Numerical / Identity / Physical) is unchanged in
  \texttt{status\_ledger.csv} --- the single source of truth --- so no fidelity is lost. The marker key,
  badge bar, README marker table and the workflow rule were updated to match.
\item \textbf{Status tables reconciled against the ledger.} The introduction's inflation/$N_\star$ rows
  are made consistent with \vref{v86}/\texttt{COSMO.NSTAR.01}: $r$ and $n_s$ are shown as the frozen
  \emph{bands} over $N_\star\in[50,60]$ with the scalaron-reheating conditional point $N_\star{=}51.4$
  ($n_s{=}0.9611$, $r{=}0.0045$), replacing the stale point values $N_\star{=}55$ (predictions table)
  and $N_\star\simeq57$ (residual card); the closure-ledger inflation row is re-typed \mE\,$\to$\,\mC
  (conditional on $M_{\rm Star}{=}M_{\rm scal}$ $+$ reheating), matching the other two tables and the
  ledger \texttt{[P]} typing.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-12 (version system, predictions/K5, readability pass B3)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Authors, auto-date and auto-version on every paper.} New single source
  \texttt{tex-artefacts/version.tex} defines \texttt{\textbackslash TFPTauthors} (Stefan Hamann,
  Alessandro Rizzo), a curated \texttt{\textbackslash TFPTversion}, and a title/footer date stamp
  (\texttt{\textbackslash today} $+$ version $+$ revision). \texttt{build.sh} writes the auto build
  revision (git commit count) into the gitignored \texttt{tex-artefacts/version-auto.tex}, so every
  document's title page and page footer carry author, date and \texttt{v\TFPTversion\,(rev~N)}
  automatically. All nine active documents and \texttt{changelog.tex} now set
  \texttt{\textbackslash author\{\textbackslash TFPTauthors\}}.
\item \textbf{Builder keeps build artefacts.} \texttt{build.sh} no longer deletes the
  \texttt{.aux/.log/.out/.toc} after a successful build (the \texttt{.log} is needed for the
  overfull-box audit and the \texttt{.aux/.toc} for correct cross-references on the next incremental
  build).
\item \textbf{Predictions table outsourced.} The running/upcoming-experiment predictions table is moved
  from \texttt{introduction.tex} into the shared fragment \texttt{tex-artefacts/predictions.tex}
  (\texttt{\textbackslash input} in the predictions section).
\item \textbf{K5 figure fixed.} The \texttt{\textbackslash TFPTactionkfive} mnemonic ($K_5$ on the five
  carrier slots) is redrawn so the complete graph and the Pascal-row reading list sit side by side
  instead of overlapping.
\item \textbf{Colour-marked script references.} New \texttt{\textbackslash vref} macro colours inline
  module references (e.g.\ \vref{v108}--\vref{v113}, \vref{v49}/\vref{v71}) in the introduction,
  predictions and verification fragments, matching the blue of the \texttt{\textbackslash veri}
  citation, so machine-checked references are visible at a glance.
\item \textbf{Lighter, non-breaking, embedded boxes.} The \texttt{tcolorbox} families are restyled to a
  light tint $+$ thin frame $+$ light title band with dark coloured title (no heavy
  white-on-saturated bars); a neutral \texttt{navbox} carries the document map and a colour-marked
  \texttt{keyeq} sets off load-bearing display formulas. The introduction's callouts use the
  non-breaking variants (\texttt{keyboxnb}/\texttt{winboxnb}/\texttt{gapboxnb}) so no box splits across
  a page, and the shared status card is non-breaking.
\item \textbf{Readability / sectioning.} The dense run-in prose of the introduction is broken into
  \texttt{\textbackslash subsection*} headings (In plain words; one anchor and $E_8$ as a compiler
  hull; the companion documents; the compact status formula; the hard reduction; the Pascal action
  grammar; the closure ledger) with added whitespace.
\item \textbf{Orphan results linked to scripts.} The Glue theorem, the ``Reduction in one line'' and the
  fermion-spectrum callouts now carry inline \texttt{\textbackslash veri\{\}} citations
  (\vref{v1}, \vref{v6}/\vref{v14}/\vref{v23}, \vref{v18}/\vref{v20}/\vref{v46}).
\end{itemize}
